# Synastry Chart SVG Example

Endpoint: `/api/v5/chart/synastry`

## Request Body
```json
{
  "first_subject": {
    "name": "Partner A",
    "year": 1990,
    "month": 1,
    "day": 1,
    "hour": 12,
    "minute": 0,
    "city": "London",
    "nation": "GB",
    "longitude": -0.1278,
    "latitude": 51.5074,
    "timezone": "Europe/London"
  },
  "second_subject": {
    "name": "Partner B",
    "year": 1992,
    "month": 5,
    "day": 15,
    "hour": 18,
    "minute": 30,
    "city": "New York",
    "nation": "US",
    "longitude": -74.006,
    "latitude": 40.7128,
    "timezone": "America/New_York"
  },
  "theme": "classic",
  "split_chart": false
}
```
